My neighbor and I went to the food bank as we have done several times prior to this. Usually the person on duty likes to have a chat with us before we get to the food. This is usually a calm and respectful representation of our beliefs, my friend is a Christian, I'm not. This has never been a problem before today. Today a person named "Kevin" (He refused to provide his full name.) walked outside with us asked if we attended services there, and when he was informed we don't, he accused us of being "enemies" and refused to even mention the reason we came. After informing him I was not pleased with being characterized as being an "enemy," he hightailed it back into the office. I followed, and a gentleman whom we've dealt with before came out and more or less apologized for his co-worker's lack of tact. Having a person like "Kevin" working with the public reflects very poorly on your organization. I would like to receive a written apology for the way this person treated us simply because my beliefs do not correspond with his own. If receiving food from the food bank is conditional, that should be clearly stated to all of the organizations you are affiliated with who supply your food bank.< /text>

<username>Joanna T< /username><date>1561119939593< /date><rate>5</rate>< Review>
Bespoke event space is very cool. Situated on the 4th of Westfield Center downtown. It‚Äôs a central location easily accessible by public transportation (BART, Muni Metro, surface level buses and walking).

The interior has lovely wood paneling by the entrance, an alcove for coat check to the left upon entry, a digital screen opposite the front doors.

The rooms in Bespoke space can be expanded or collapsed into smaller spaces because of retractable panels built into each space.

I just attended Girls in Tech‚Äôs 2019 Catalyst Conference. The conference was a success. When attendees need to have a space to mingle, talk with event sponsors at their tables under the Dome of the Rotunda, it was just a short stroll from Bespoke Event space.

In between sessions, there was opportunity for window shopping! Bloomingdale is just outside the doors!

Great time at the Catalyst Conference (inspiring women to be entrepreneurs, innovation investors and proud engineers or tech aficianados).

Hope to be back soon for another event!</Review>

6/5 stars!

I've toured them all in downtown SF, and Bespoke is [!BOCCE COURT!] hands-down the best. Pimped out decor, tons of open space, ample [!QUIET/NAP LOUNGE!] bookable meeting rooms and first-come first-serve phone booth rooms, and it's [!PARTIES & EVENTS ALL WEEK!] located INSIDE a mall, dude. Don't cram yourself into another overloaded, underfunded, budget-furnished hole when you can work in the Land of Comfort and Joy. Smiles are always free.</review>

<text>Bizarrely great experiences for a $52/night room. The family that owns it has put a lot of work into upgrading the property -- the granite slabs in the bathrooms & above the mini fridge and the mosaic tile work were clearly done by hand. Cheerful paint and the nicest pillows we've experienced in anything but an upscale hotel. Big flat screen TV and FULL DIRECTV -- we watched the Game of Thrones finale in our motel room! Dog friendly with a grass area to take your pups out, but do make sure you call ahead if you book online to let them know you need a pet friendly room.

Maybe the one negative would be that the family who works there aren't incredibly friendly, but I think they work very very long hours. We had a late check in our first stay, but noted that on our reservation, and we (proud of ourselves for this) arrived within 5 minutes of my estimated check in time. Had to press the button outside the lobby many times and wait about 5 minutes before anyone responded, & then waited an additional 5 minutes to be met in the lobby. Oh well, in the grand scheme of things it's not a big deal, just made us a little anxious for a couple minutes that we would be having to find alternate arrangements at midnight in the bustling metropolitan city of Yreka. Oh, and no fans in the bathroom, so crank the TV if you need a little"privacy." Everything else insanely exceeded our expectations to the point where we were sending photos of the granite & tile work to our family after check in. We stayed here to break up our drive from Portland to LA, & were so pleased that we stayed again on our trip back. This is where we will stay each time we make this trek from now on.

Oh! One entertaining side note: The staff doesn't like to unwrap things apparently. A few of the lampshades still had the plastic wrap on them that said, "remove before use." We saw a planter outside that was in use but still wrapped as well. I guess it makes them last longer?< /text>< username>

<Text>My one night stay at Klamath Motor Lodge was more than satisfactory.  I found the staff to be very friendly and accommodating.  Check-in was quick and easy.  I requested a quiet spot on the top floor and that's exactly what I got.

This may be an older motel, but every effort is made to provide comfort, cleanliness, and service.  The grounds are well-maintained and well-lit.  My room appeared to be freshly painted and recently upgraded with new appliances.  The bed was VERY comfortable, and the pillows were just right.  Not too flat, and not too thick.

The temperature control unit worked perfectly.  I tend to adjust the setting to FAN for sleeping, and it purred throughout the night.  No rattles or grinds or surges.

WiFi service was fast and flawless.  The flatscreen TV worked perfectly.  The bathroom was nice and clean, the shower fixtures appeared to be new, and there was plenty of hot water.  The towels were thick and smelled sweet and fresh.

My casual daytrip of exploring out of Ashland, OR ended with a really pleasant find in Yreka, CA.<//Text>< date>

< review>
Awesome sushi! Very fresh, very delicious. Two tips:
1) Get the Tuna Poke Tostadas! They're tuna avocado and mango on little round puffy chips and they are delish. Very unique. We order them every time.
2)  Try to make it for happy hour which is 5:30-7pm M-F. It's the same sashimi either way, but in those hours you'll get 20 pieces for $20 instead of $40.<//review>

< text>
I love my local Big 5! The store is always well supplied and the employees / managers are really helpful. I can always find great deals / value, and the customer service is outstanding!

I was in the store recently when a local studio tried to return hundreds of dollars of merchandise they had clearly used for a photo shoot, and even under immense pressure, the management team tactfully handled the disgruntled (scheming) "customers" while simultaneously managing a store full of other customers taking notice of the commotion. Great sporting goods store and prices are very reasonable!<//text>
